data-feature="TabbedListButton" data-feature-variant="Right" data-index="2">Nutrition</button></h2></div><div class="tabbed-list__content"><div class=""><section id="ingredients-list" class="ingredients-list" data-component="IngredientsList" data-feature="Recipe Instructions" data-stitcher-dai-container="ingredients-list"><section><ul class="ingredients-list list"><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item">180g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/prawn-glossary" data-component="Link">pack peeled raw prawns</a><div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> roughly chopped</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">4 <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/salmon-glossary" data-component="Link">skinless salmon</a><div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> fillets, chopped into small chunks</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">3 <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/spring-onion-glossary" data-component="Link">spring onions</a><div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> roughly chopped</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">1 <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/lemon-glossary" data-component="Link">lemon</a><div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> zested and juiced</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">small pack coriander</li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">60g <!-- -->mayonnaise<div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> or Greek yogurt</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">4 tsp <!-- -->chilli sauce<div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> (we used sriracha)</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">2 <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/lettuce-glossary" data-component="Link">Little Gem lettuces</a><div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> shredded</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">1 <!-- -->cucumber<div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> peeled into ribbons</div></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">1 tbsp <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/olive-oil-glossary" data-component="Link">olive oil</a></li><li class="ingredients-list__item list-item list-item--separator-top">4 <!-- -->seeded burger buns<div class="ingredients-list__item-note"> toasted, to serve</div></li></ul></section></section></div><div class="d-none"><p class="recipe__nutritions-caption">Nutrition: Per serving</p><ul class="nutrition-list"><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">kcal</span>504</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">fat</span>36<!-- -->g</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">saturates</span>5<!-- -->g</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">carbs</span>4<!-- -->g</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">sugars</span>4<!-- -->g</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">fibre</span>3<!-- -->g</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">protein</span>39<!-- -->g</li><li class="nutrition-list__item"><span class="fw-600 mr-1">salt</span>0.7<!-- -->g</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="ad-slot__text">Ad</span></div><div id="recipe--below-ingredients--1" class="ad-unit"></div></div><div><script>(window.adq = window.adq || []).push((api) => api.addSlot({"key":"below-ingredients","index":1,"searchTerm":null,"fullSearchTerm":null}));</script></div></div><div class="js-piano-recipe-method col-12 pa-reset"><section class="method-steps mb-lg" data-placement="MethodList"><h2 class="method-steps__heading heading-3">Method</h2><ul class="method-steps__list"><li class="method-steps__list-item"><h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 1</h3><div class="editor-content"><p>Briefly blitz half the prawns, half the salmon, the spring onions, lemon zest and half the coriander in a <a href="https://www.bbcgoodfood.com/content/test-five-best-food-processors">food processor</a> until it forms a coarse paste. Tip into a bowl, stir in the rest of the prawns and salmon, season well and shape into four burgers. Chill for 10 mins.</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="277"></div></div></li><li class="method-steps__list-item"><h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 2</h3><div class="editor-content"><p>Mix the mayo and chilli sauce together in a small bowl, season and add some lemon juice to taste. Mix the lettuce with the cucumber, dress with a little of the remaining lemon juice and 1 tsp olive oil, then set aside.</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="501"></div></div></li><li class="method-steps__list-item"><h3 class="method-steps__item-heading heading-5">step 3</h3><div class="editor-content"><p>Heat the remaining oil in a large <a href="https://www.bbcgoodfood.com/content/top-five-non-stick-frying-pans">frying pan</a> and fry the burgers for 3-4 mins each side or until they have a nice crust and the fish is cooked through. Serve with the salad on the side or in toasted burger buns, if you like, with a good dollop of the spicy mayo.</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="769"></div></div></li></ul></section></div></div></div></div><div class="post__content-end row hidden-print"><div class="col-12"></div></div><p class="post__publication-link hidden-print">Recipe from Good Food magazine, <!-- -->July 2017</p></div><div class="ad-slot hidden-print mb-lg hidden-for-md hidden-for-lg ad-slot--bordered"><div class="ad-slot__container"><div
